respawn via stable wrapper after self-update\",\"body\":\"Fixes #52313\\n\\n## Summary\\n- rewrite self-respawn entrypoints to prefer a stable OpenClaw entrypoint instead of blindly reusing the current argv path\\n- special-case pnpm versioned realpaths so restart/update can come back through a stable package path\\n- preserve source-checkout restarts via `scripts/run-node.mjs` so repo-based dev runs keep their build wrapper\\n- preserve the original runtime cwd when source-checkout restarts hand off through `scripts/run-node.mjs`\\n- preserve source-checkout Node `execArgv` and `NODE_OPTIONS` across both the rebuild child and the final `openclaw.mjs` child without double-binding inspector/debug-port flags, double-running preload modules on the intermediate wrapper process, or leaving the one-shot rebuild child stuck in `--watch*` mode\\n- anchor source-checkout git-head checks and `.buildstamp` writes to the wrapper package root instead of the preserved runtime cwd\\n- keep dev/source entrypoints unchanged\\n- keep Bun-packaged gateways on stable `dist/*` entrypoints instead of rewriting them to `openclaw.mjs`\\n- make the new respawn assertions cross-platform so Windows runners validate the same behavior\\n\\n## Why\\n`restartGatewayProcessWithFreshPid()` previously spawned the child from `process.execArgv + process.argv.slice(1)`.\\nThat is fragile after self-update when the running process was launched from a package-manager-managed realpath, because the parent can exit cleanly and the child can be pointed at an entrypoint that no longer exists.\\n\\nIt also bypassed the repo `scripts/run-node.mjs` wrapper when a source checkout restarted from `openclaw.mjs`, which could skip the rebuild path that dev checkouts rely on. And when the checkout was launched from outside the repo root, `scripts/run-node.mjs` needed the package root for build/dist resolution while the actual runtime still needed the original cwd. Once restarts started flowing through that wrapper, both the rebuild step and the final `openclaw.mjs` launch needed to retain the original Node runtime flags, while debugger-specific flags such as `--inspect*` must not bind on the intermediate wrapper process and preload flags such as `--import` / `--require` must not execute twice there. The wrapper also has to keep git-head checks and build-stamp writes anchored to the package root rather than the preserved runtime cwd, or out-of-tree restarts can miss stale-build detection and write stamps to the wrong `dist/` tree.\\n\\n## Implementation\\n- detect pnpm realpaths under `node_modules/.pnpm/.../node_modules/openclaw/...` and rewrite them to a stable package entrypoint\\n- when running from a source checkout under Node, prefer `\\u003cpackageRoot\\u003e/scripts/run-node.mjs` so restarts preserve the build wrapper\\n- keep source-checkout respawns on the original runtime cwd so relative paths still resolve exactly as they did before restart\\n- update `scripts/run-node.mjs` to derive the package root from its own wrapper path, then exec an absolute `openclaw.mjs` back in the original runtime cwd\\n- forward the original `execArgv` and `NODE_OPTIONS` to `scripts/run-node.mjs`, but strip inspector/debug-port and preload-only flags from the intermediate wrapper hop so the final gateway process owns the debugger session and preload side effects only run once\\n- restore the forwarded `execArgv` and `NODE_OPTIONS` for both `scripts/tsdown-build.mjs` and the final `\\u003cpackageRoot\\u003e/openclaw.mjs` child so rebuild-required restarts keep the same Node runtime configuration end-to-end, while stripping `--watch*` from the one-shot rebuild step so it can still finish and relaunch\\n- resolve git heads and write `.buildstamp` files from the wrapper package root even when the runtime cwd is external to the checkout\\n- when running under Bun, prefer a stable built `dist/*` entrypoint at the package root\\n- otherwise, if the OpenClaw package root is known, respawn via `\\u003cpackageRoot\\u003e/openclaw.mjs` and fall back to built `dist/*` entries when needed\\n- preserve the current argv for direct dev/source entrypoints such as `src/entry.ts`\\n- add focused tests for package-root respawn, pnpm path rewriting, Bun compatibility, source-checkout wrapper preservation, runtime-cwd preservation, debugger-safe `execArgv` forwarding, preload-safe forwarding, rebuild-child flag forwarding, package-root git-head/build-stamp anchoring, pnpm-linked source-tree wrapper forwarding, dev-mode passthrough, and cross-platform path expectations\\n\\n## Validation\\n- `pnpm test -- src/infra/process-respawn.test.ts src/infra/run-node.test.ts`\\n- `pnpm exec oxlint --type-aware src/infra/process-respawn.ts src/infra/process-respawn.test.ts src/infra/run-node.test.ts scripts/run-node.mjs`\\n- `pnpm exec oxfmt --check src/infra/process-respawn.ts src/infra/process-respawn.test.ts src/infra/run-node.test.ts scripts/run-node.mjs`\\n- local `git commit` pre-commit suite passed on this head\\n\\n## Base\\nI `c1d76478ded448305e33e9484b12c9183d3fb468`\\n- newer `main` commits must still be re-checked for full-matrix green status before any further PR
